Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageKisco Senior Living contact form
URLhttps://www.kiscoseniorliving.com/contact/
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro

Score1207
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1207, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 145. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 100. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

solos: Score 72. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 224

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r69, score 112 (Text outside widget has subminimum contrast)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 77 (Element has insufficient color contrast)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G18.Fail, score 12 (Contrast between the text and its background is less than 4.5:1)
  • Package ibm, test IBMA_Color_Contrast_WCAG2AA, score 108 (Contrast ratio of text with background does not meet WCAG 2.1 AA)
  • Package wave, test c:contrast, score 78 (Very low contrast)

Issue contentBeyondLandmarks

WCAG: 1.3.6

Score: 71

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r57, score 62 (Perceivable text content is not included in any landmark)
  • Package axe, test region, score 2 (Some page content is not contained by landmarks)
  • Package ibm, test Rpt_Aria_OrphanedContent_Native_Host_Sematics, score 16 (Content does not reside within an element with a landmark role)

Issue contrastAAA

WCAG: 1.4.6

Score: 71

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r66, score 53 (Text contrast less than AAA requires)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast-enhanced, score 15 (Element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G17.Fail, score 24 (Text has insufficient contrast)

Issue hoverSurprise

WCAG: 1.4.13

Score: 62

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test hover, score 60 (Hovering is mis-indicated or changes content)

Issue linkIndication

WCAG: 1.3.3

Score: 45

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test linkUl, score 43 (Non-underlined adjacent links)

Issue linkNoText

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 44

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r11, score 16 (Link has no accessible name)
  • Package continuum, test 237, score 16 (a element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name value to be calculated)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.4_1_2.H91.A.NoContent, score 16 (Link has an href attribute but no text)
  • Package wave, test e:link_empty, score 16 (Link contains no text)
  • Package tenon, test 57, score 16 (Link has no text inside it)
